* [28 February 2020](https://web.archive.org/web/20200228172210/https://twitter.com/RonColeman/status/1233428152946450433) ([live](https://twitter.com/RonColeman/status/1233436714745696256)): Which state's law should apply is a very complex and technical matter. As you can guess based on which side wants which state's law to apply, Alabama law is more protective of the right not to be defamed than New York's law, known to be very tough on defamation plaintiffs.
* [28 February 2020](https://web.archive.org/web/20200228172210/https://twitter.com/RonColeman/status/1233428152946450433) ([live](https://twitter.com/RonColeman/status/1233436044181299200)): The Palin ruling bears on Gavin's claims in numerous respects, and it is of particular interest because one of the disputes before the judge is whether Alabama law applies (as we say it does) or New York law does (as SPLC says).
